local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local CoreGui = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local function MinimalNotify(text)
    local targetParent = (run_secure_function and CoreGui) or (gethui and gethui()) or Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui")
    if not targetParent then return end
    local sg = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    sg.Name = "MinimalErrorProtect"
    sg.ResetOnSpawn = false
    sg.Parent = targetParent
    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 15, 15)
    frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, -350, 0, 20)
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 0)
    frame.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    frame.Parent = sg
    local uic = Instance.new("UICorner")
    uic.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
    uic.Parent = frame
    local padding = Instance.new("UIPadding")
    padding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 10)
    padding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 10)
    padding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 12)
    padding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 12)
    padding.Parent = frame
    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.Text = tostring(text)
    lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
    lbl.TextSize = 16
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0)
    lbl.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    lbl.TextWrapped = true
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.Parent = frame
    local slideIn = TweenService:Create(frame, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
        Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
    })
    local slideOut = TweenService:Create(frame, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
        Position = UDim2.new(0, -350, 0, 20)
    })

    slideIn:Play()
    task.delay(4, function()
        if frame and sg then
            slideOut:Play()
            slideOut.Completed:Wait()
            sg:Destroy()
        end
    end)
end

local function bp(code)
    local func, syntaxErr = loadstring(code)
    if not func then
        local cleanErr = syntaxErr:gsub("^.-:%d+: ", "")
        MinimalNotify("Syntax Error:\n" .. cleanErr)
        return
    end
    local success, runtimeErr = pcall(func)
    if not success then
        local cleanErr = runtimeErr:gsub("^.-:%d+: ", "")
        MinimalNotify("Runtime Error:\n" .. cleanErr)
    end
end

bp(i)

        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(220, 130, 255)),
    })
    progressFillGrad.Rotation = 0
    progressFillGrad.Parent = progressFill

    -- ── FOOTER ────────────────────────────────────────────
    local footerLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    footerLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 18)
    footerLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 448)
    footerLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    footerLbl.Text = "LZ7 Team  •  youtube.com/@LZ7  •  v3.0"
    footerLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 65, 110)
    footerLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    footerLbl.TextSize = 9
    footerLbl.ZIndex = 3
    footerLbl.Parent = card

    -- ── ATTEMPT COUNTER ───────────────────────────────────
    local attemptCount = 0
    local maxAttempts = 5

    local attemptLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    attemptLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 14)
    attemptLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 432)
    attemptLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    attemptLbl.Text = ""
    attemptLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 80, 140)
    attemptLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    attemptLbl.TextSize = 10
    attemptLbl.ZIndex = 3
    attemptLbl.Parent = card

    -- ── ANIMAÇÃO DE ENTRADA ───────────────────────────────
    card.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -210, 0.5, -240)
    card.BackgroundTransparency = 1

    -- Fade + scale in
    local function animateIn()
        local elements = {
            titleLabel, versionBadge, divider, keyTitleGroup,
            inputWrapper, verifyBtn, statusFrame, footerLbl, attemptLbl
        }
        for _, el in ipairs(elements) do
            if el:IsA("Frame") or el:IsA("TextLabel") or el:IsA("TextButton") then
                el.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            end
        end

        TweenService:Create(card, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
            BackgroundTransparency = 0,
        }):Play()
        TweenService:Create(overlay, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.45
        }):Play()

        task.wait(0.1)

        TweenService:Create(inputWrapper, TweenInfo.new(0.35), {
            BackgroundTransparency = 0
        }):Play()
        TweenService:Create(verifyBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.35), {
            BackgroundTransparency = 0
        }):Play()
    end

    task.spawn(animateIn)

    -- ── ANIMAÇÃO DO ORBE ──────────────────────────────────
    task.spawn(function()
        while card.Parent do
            TweenService:Create(glowOuter, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
                ImageTransparency = 0.45,
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 170, 0, 170),
                Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -85, 0, 15)
            }):Play()
            TweenService:Create(logoRing, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(190, 80, 250)
            }):Play()
            task.wait(2)
            TweenService:Create(glowOuter, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
                ImageTransparency = 0.7,
                Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 150),
                Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -75, 0, 25)
            }):Play()
            TweenService:Create(logoRing, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
                BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 50, 210)
            }):Play()
            task.wait(2)
        end
    end)

    -- ── ANIMAÇÃO DA BARRA SUPERIOR ────────────────────────
    task.spawn(function()
        while card.Parent do
            TweenService:Create(topBarGrad, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {
                Offset = Vector2.new(0.5, 0)
            }):Play()
            task.wait(2)
            TweenService:Create(topBarGrad, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {
                Offset = Vector2.new(-0.5, 0)
            }):Play()
            task.wait(2)
        end
    end)

    -- ── BORDA PULSANTE ────────────────────────────────────
    task.spawn(function()
        while card.Parent do
            TweenService:Create(cardStroke, TweenInfo.new(1.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {
                Transparency = 0.5,
                Thickness = 1
            }):Play()
            task.wait(1.5)
            TweenService:Create(cardStroke, TweenInfo.new(1.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {
                Transparency = 0,
                Thickness = 2
            }):Play()
            task.wait(1.5)
        end
    end)

    -- ── LÓGICA DO BOTÃO ───────────────────────────────────
    local function setStatus(icon, msg, color)
        statusIcon.Text = icon
        statusMsg.Text = msg
        statusMsg.TextColor3 = color
    end

    local function playProgressBar(duration, onDone)
        progressBg.Visible = true
        progressFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
        TweenService:Create(progressFill, TweenInfo.new(duration, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {
            Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        }):Play()
        task.delay(duration, onDone)
    end

    local isVerifying = false

    local function doVerify()
        if isVerifying then return end
        isVerifying = true

        local inputKey = keyBox.Text

        -- Estado: verificando
        verifyLbl.Text = "⏳  VERIFYING..."
        verifyBtn.Active = false
        setStatus("", "", Color3.new())

        playProgressBar(0.8, function()
            if inputKey == WHITELIST_KEY then
                -- ✅ SUCESSO
                progressFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 220, 140)
                local fillGrad = progressFill:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIGradient")
                if fillGrad then
                    fillGrad.Color = ColorSequence.new({
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(80, 220, 140)),
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(150, 255, 200)),
                    })
                end

                verifyLbl.Text = "✓  ACCESS GRANTED"
                setStatus("✅", "Authenticated successfully!", Color3.fromRGB(80, 220, 140))

                TweenService:Create(cardStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
                    Color = Color3.fromRGB(80, 220, 140),
                    Transparency = 0
                }):Play()
                TweenService:Create(topBar, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
                    BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 220, 140)
                }):Play()

                local notifSuccess, _ = pcall(function()
                    game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                        Title = "LZ7 BLOX V3.0",
                        Text = "✅ Authenticated successfully!",
                        Duration = 3,
                        Icon = "rbxassetid://131866225863044"
                    })
                end)

                task.wait(1.2)

                -- Animação de saída
                TweenService:Create(card, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
                    BackgroundTransparency = 1,
                    Size = UDim2.new(0, 380, 0, 440),
                    Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -190, 0.5, -220)
                }):Play()
                TweenService:Create(overlay, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
                    BackgroundTransparency = 1
                }):Play()

                task.wait(0.45)
                isAuthenticated = true
                authGui:Destroy()

            else
                -- ❌ ERRO
                attemptCount = attemptCount + 1
                local remaining = maxAttempts - attemptCount

                progressFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 100)
                local fillGrad = progressFill:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIGradient")
                if fillGrad then
                    fillGrad.Color = ColorSequence.new({
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 100)),
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 140, 160)),
                    })
                end

                verifyLbl.Text = "✗  ACCESS DENIED"
                setStatus("❌", "Invalid key! " .. remaining .. " attempts left.", Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 100))

                attemptLbl.Text = "Attempts: " .. attemptCount .. " / " .. maxAttempts

                -- Shake animation
                local origPos = card.Position
                for i = 1, 6 do
                    local offset = (i % 2 == 0) and 8 or -8
                    TweenService:Create(card, TweenInfo.new(0.05), {
                        Position = UDim2.new(origPos.X.Scale, origPos.X.Offset + offset, origPos.Y.Scale, origPos.Y.Offset)
                    }):Play()
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
                TweenService:Create(card, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
                    Position = origPos
                }):Play()

                -- Flash borda vermelha
                TweenService:Create(cardStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {
                    Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 100),
                    Transparency = 0
                }):Play()
                task.wait(0.6)
                TweenService:Create(cardStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
                    Color = Color3.fromRGB(170, 60, 230),
                    Transparency = 0.2
                }):Play()

                pcall(function()
                    game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                        Title = "LZ7 BLOX V3.0",
                        Text = "❌ Invalid key! " .. remaining .. " attempts left.",
                        Duration = 2,
                        Icon = "rbxassetid://131866225863044"
                    })
                end)

                keyBox.Text = ""
                keyBox.PlaceholderText = "Wrong key, try again..."

                -- Reset botão
                task.wait(0.5)
                verifyLbl.Text = "✓  VERIFY ACCESS"
                verifyBtn.Active = true
                progressBg.Visible = false

                -- Se excedeu tentativas
                if attemptCount >= maxAttempts then
                    setStatus("🚫", "Too many attempts. Closing...", Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 100))
                    verifyBtn.Active = false
                    task.wait(2.5)
                    TweenService:Create(card, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
                        BackgroundTransparency = 1
                    }):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(overlay, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {
                        BackgroundTransparency = 1
                    }):Play()
                    task.wait(0.5)
                    authGui:Destroy()
                end

                isVerifying = false
                return
            end
            isVerifying = false
        end)
    end

    verifyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(doVerify)

    keyBox.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
        if enterPressed then
            doVerify()
        end
    end)

    repeat task.wait() until isAuthenticated == true
end

task.spawn(function()
    checkWhitelist()
    task.wait(0.5)
end)

-- Aguarda autenticação antes de continuar
while not isAuthenticated do
    task.wait()
end

local function tween(obj, props, duration, style, dir)
    local info = TweenInfo.new(
        duration or 0.25,
        style or Enum.EasingStyle.Quint,
        dir or Enum.EasingDirection.Out
    )
    local t = TweenService:Create(obj, info, props)
    t:Play()
    return t
end

local function corner(parent, radius)
    local c = Instance.new("UICorner")
    c.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, radius or 8)
    c.Parent = parent
    return c
end

local function stroke(parent, color, thickness, transparency)
    local s = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    s.Color = color or Theme.border
    s.Thickness = thickness or 1
    s.Transparency = transparency or 0
    s.ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
    s.Parent = parent
    return s
end

local function gradient(parent, colors, rotation)
    local g = Instance.new("UIGradient")
    g.Color = ColorSequence.new(colors)
    g.Rotation = rotation or 90
    g.Parent = parent
    return g
end

local function shadow(parent, transparency)
    local s = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
    s.Name = "Shadow"
    s.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
    s.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    s.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
    s.Size = UDim2.new(1, 24, 1, 24)
    s.Image = "rbxassetid://6014261993"
    s.ImageColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
    s.ImageTransparency = transparency or 0.5
    s.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Slice
    s.SliceCenter = Rect.new(49, 49, 450, 450)
    s.ZIndex = parent.ZIndex - 1
    s.Parent = parent
    return s
end

local function ripple(button)
    button.ClipsDescendants = true
    button.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function(x, y)
        local r = Instance.new("Frame")
        r.Name = "Ripple"
        r.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
        r.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.text
        r.BackgroundTransparency = 0.7
        r.BorderSizePixel = 0
        r.Position = UDim2.new(0, x - button.AbsolutePosition.X, 0, y - button.AbsolutePosition.Y)
        r.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        r.ZIndex = button.ZIndex + 1
        r.Parent = button
        corner(r, 100)
        local maxSize = math.max(button.AbsoluteSize.X, button.AbsoluteSize.Y) * 2
        tween(r, {Size = UDim2.new(0, maxSize, 0, maxSize), BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.5)
        game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(r, 0.5)
    end)
end

    end)
end)

local function toggleCursor()
    cursorUnlocked = not cursorUnlocked
    UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = cursorUnlocked
    UserInputService.MouseBehavior = cursorUnlocked and Enum.MouseBehavior.Default or Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter
    CONFIG.cursorUnlocked = cursorUnlocked
end

UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gp)
    if not gp and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.P then
        toggleCursor()
    end
end)

local function canSeeTarget(character)
    if not CONFIG.aimWallCheck then return true end
    if not (localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")) then return false end
    if not (character and character:FindFirstChild("Head")) then return false end
    local origin = localPlayer.Character.Head.Position
    local target = character.Head.Position
    local direction = (target - origin).Unit
    local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
    raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Blacklist
    raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {localPlayer.Character, character}
    local rayResult = Workspace:Raycast(origin + direction * 3, direction * (target - origin).Magnitude, raycastParams)
    return rayResult == nil
end

local function isValidTarget(player)
    if player == localPlayer then return false end
    if not player.Character then return false end
    local humanoid = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 then return false end
    if not player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then return false end
    if CONFIG.teamCheck and player.Team == localPlayer.Team then return false end
    return true
end

local function getClosestTarget()
    local target = nil
    local shortestDist = CONFIG.aimFOV
    local center = Vector2.new(Camera.ViewportSize.X / 2, Camera.ViewportSize.Y / 2)
    if not (localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")) then return nil end
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if isValidTarget(player) then
            local head = player.Character.Head
            local pos, onScreen = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(head.Position)
            if onScreen then
                if CONFIG.aimWallCheck and not canSeeTarget(player.Character) then continue end
                local screenPos = Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)
                local dist = (screenPos - center).Magnitude
                if dist < shortestDist then
                    shortestDist = dist
                    target = player.Character
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return target
end

local function updateBacktrackHistory()
    if not CONFIG.backtrackEnabled then return end
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            local head = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if hrp and head then
                if not backtrackHistory[player] then backtrackHistory[player] = {} end
                table.insert(backtrackHistory[player], {
                    position = hrp.Position,
                    headPosition = head.Position,
                    cframe = hrp.CFrame,
                    time = tick()
                })
                while #backtrackHistory[player] > CONFIG.backtrackTicks do
                    table.remove(backtrackHistory[player], 1)
                end
                local currentTime = tick()
                for i = #backtrackHistory[player], 1, -1 do
                    if currentTime - backtrackHistory[player][i].time > CONFIG.backtrackTime then
                        table.remove(backtrackHistory[player], i)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

local function getBestBacktrackPosition(target)
    if not CONFIG.backtrackEnabled then return nil end
    if not backtrackHistory[target] then return nil end
    if #backtrackHistory[target] == 0 then return nil end
    local bestPosition = nil
    local bestDistance = math.huge
    local center = Vector2.new(Camera.ViewportSize.X / 2, Camera.ViewportSize.Y / 2)
    for _, record in ipairs(backtrackHistory[target]) do
        local pos, onScreen = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(record.headPosition)
        if onScreen then
            local screenDist = (Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y) - center).Magnitude
            if screenDist < bestDistance then
                bestDistance = screenDist
                bestPosition = record
            end
        end
    end
    return bestPosition
end

local function drawBacktrackIndicators()
    if not CONFIG.backtrackEnabled or not CONFIG.backtrackIndicator then return end
    for player, history in pairs(backtrackHistory) do
        if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and player.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
            for i, record in ipairs(history) do
                local pos, onScreen = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(record.headPosition)
                if onScreen then
                    local alpha = 1 - (i / #history) * 0.7
                    if not backtrackIndicators[player] then backtrackIndicators[player] = {} end
                    if not backtrackIndicators[player][i] then
                        backtrackIndicators[player][i] = Drawing.new("Circle")
                        backtrackIndicators[player][i].Radius = 5
                        backtrackIndicators[player][i].Thickness = 1.5
                        backtrackIndicators[player][i].Filled = false
                        backtrackIndicators[player][i].Color = Color3.fromRGB(180, 120, 255)
                    end
                    local indicator = backtrackIndicators[player][i]
                    indicator.Visible = true
                    indicator.Position = Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)
                    indicator.Transparency = alpha
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

local function handleAimbot()
    if not CONFIG.aimEnabled then return end
    local target = getClosestTarget()
    if not target then return end
    if CONFIG.silentAimEnabled then return end
    local shouldAim = false
    local aimPart = nil
    if CONFIG.aimKey == "F" then
        if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.F) then aimPart = target:FindFirstChild("Head"); shouldAim = true end
    elseif CONFIG.aimKey == "V" then
        if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.V) then aimPart = target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"); shouldAim = true end
    elseif CONFIG.aimKey == "always" then
        aimPart = target:FindFirstChild("Head"); shouldAim = true
    elseif CONFIG.aimKey == "MouseButton2" then
        if UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then aimPart = target:FindFirstChild("Head"); shouldAim = true end
    end
    if shouldAim and aimPart then
        local targetPos = aimPart.Position
        if CONFIG.backtrackEnabled then
            local backtrackPos = getBestBacktrackPosition(target.Parent)
            if backtrackPos then targetPos = backtrackPos.headPosition end
        end
        local targetCFrame = CFrame.new(Camera.CFrame.Position, targetPos)
        local smoothFactor = CONFIG.smoothness / 100
        Camera.CFrame = Camera.CFrame:Lerp(targetCFrame, smoothFactor)
    end
end

local function modifyShot()
    if not CONFIG.silentAimEnabled or not CONFIG.aimEnabled then return end
    local target = getClosestTarget()
    if not target then return end
    local targetPosition = nil
    if target:FindFirstChild("Head") then
        targetPosition = target.Head.Position
    elseif target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        targetPosition = target.HumanoidRootPart.Position
    else return end
    if CONFIG.backtrackEnabled then
        local backtrackPos = getBestBacktrackPosition(target.Parent)
        if backtrackPos then targetPosition = backtrackPos.headPosition end
    end
    local cameraPos = Camera.CFrame.Position
    local direction = (targetPosition - cameraPos).Unit
    local targetCFrame = CFrame.new(cameraPos, cameraPos + direction)
    local originalCFrame = Camera.CFrame
    Camera.CFrame = targetCFrame
    task.wait(0.01)
    Camera.CFrame = originalCFrame
end

local function setupSilentAim()
    if silentAimConnection then silentAimConnection:Disconnect() end
    silentAimConnection = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gp)
        if gp then return end
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            if CONFIG.silentAimEnabled and CONFIG.aimEnabled then
                task.spawn(modifyShot)
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function startFakeLag()
    if fakeLagConnection then fakeLagConnection:Disconnect() end
    if not CONFIG.fakeLagEnabled then return end
    if not localPlayer.Character then return end
    local hrp = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    lastPosition = hrp.Position
    fakeLagConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        if not CONFIG.fakeLagEnabled or not localPlayer.Character then return end
        local h = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not h then return end
        lagTimer = lagTimer + dt
        if lagTimer >= CONFIG.fakeLagDelay then
            lagTimer = 0
            if CONFIG.fakeLagMode == "Teleport" and lastPosition then
                local current = h.Position
                h.CFrame = CFrame.new(lastPosition) * CFrame.Angles(0, h.Orientation.Y, 0)
                lastPosition = current
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function stopFakeLag()
    if fakeLagConnection then fakeLagConnection:Disconnect(); fakeLagConnection = nil end
    lagTimer = 0
end

local function updateESP()
    if not CONFIG.espEnabled then
        for _, esp in pairs(espTable) do
            for _, drawing in pairs(esp) do
                pcall(function() drawing.Visible = false end)
            end
        end
        return
    end
    if not (localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then return end
    local myPos = localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if isValidTarget(player) then
            local char = player.Character
            local hrp = char.HumanoidRootPart
            local head = char.Head
            local dist = (myPos - hrp.Position).Magnitude
            if dist <= CONFIG.espDistance then
                local hrpPos, onScreen = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(hrp.Position)
                local headPos = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(head.Position)
                if onScreen then
                    if not espTable[player] then
                        espTable[player] = {}
                        espTable[player].Box = Drawing.new("Square")
                        espTable[player].Box.Thickness = 1.5
                        espTable[player].Box.Color = Theme.accent
                        espTable[player].Tracer = Drawing.new("Line")
                        espTable[player].Tracer.Thickness = 1.5
                        espTable[player].Tracer.Color = Theme.accent
                        espTable[player].Name = Drawing.new("Text")
                        espTable[player].Name.Size = 14
                        espTable[player].Name.Center = true
                        espTable[player].Name.Outline = true
                        espTable[player].Name.OutlineColor = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
                        espTable[player].Name.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
                        espTable[player].HealthBg = Drawing.new("Square")
                        espTable[player].HealthBg.Filled = true
                        espTable[player].HealthBg.Color = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
                        espTable[player].HealthBg.Transparency = 0.5
                        espTable[player].Health = Drawing.new("Square")
                        espTable[player].Health.Filled = true
                    end
                    local esp = espTable[player]
                    local boxHeight = math.abs(hrpPos.Y - headPos.Y) * 2
                    local boxWidth = boxHeight * 0.6
                    local boxX = hrpPos.X - boxWidth / 2
                    local boxY = headPos.Y - boxHeight * 0.1
                    esp.Box.Visible = CONFIG.espBox
                    if CONFIG.espBox then
                        esp.Box.Position = Vector2.new(boxX, boxY)
                        esp.Box.Size = Vector2.new(boxWidth, boxHeight)
                    end
                    esp.Tracer.Visible = CONFIG.espTracer
                    if CONFIG.espTracer then
                        esp.Tracer.From = Vector2.new(Camera.ViewportSize.X / 2, Camera.ViewportSize.Y)
                        esp.Tracer.To = Vector2.new(hrpPos.X, hrpPos.Y)
                    end
                    esp.Name.Visible = CONFIG.espName
                    if CONFIG.espName then
                        esp.Name.Position = Vector2.new(hrpPos.X, boxY - 18)
                        esp.Name.Text = player.Name .. " [" .. math.floor(dist) .. "m]"
                    end
                    if CONFIG.espHealth then
                        local healthPercent = char.Humanoid.Health / char.Humanoid.MaxHealth
                        esp.HealthBg.Visible = true
                        esp.HealthBg.Position = Vector2.new(boxX - 8, boxY)
                        esp.HealthBg.Size = Vector2.new(4, boxHeight)
                        esp.Health.Visible = true
                        esp.Health.Position = Vector2.new(boxX - 8, boxY + boxHeight * (1 - healthPercent))
                        esp.Health.Size = Vector2.new(4, boxHeight * healthPercent)
                        esp.Health.Color = Color3.new(1 - healthPercent, healthPercent, 0)
                    else
                        esp.HealthBg.Visible = false
                        esp.Health.Visible = false
                    end
                elseif espTable[player] then
                    for _, d in pairs(espTable[player]) do d.Visible = false end
                end
            elseif espTable[player] then
                for _, d in pairs(espTable[player]) do d.Visible = false end
            end
        elseif espTable[player] then
            for _, d in pairs(espTable[player]) do d.Visible = false end
        end
    end
end

local function createWatermark()
    if watermarkGui then watermarkGui:Destroy() end
    watermarkGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    watermarkGui.Name = "LZ7Watermark"
    watermarkGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    watermarkGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
    watermarkGui.Parent = playerGui
    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 180, 0, 32)
    frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
    frame.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgPanel
    frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    frame.Parent = watermarkGui
    corner(frame, 8)
    stroke(frame, Theme.accent, 1, 0.4)
    local icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
    icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22)
    icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0.5, -11)
    icon.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent
    icon.BorderSizePixel = 0
    icon.Image = LZ7_ICON
    icon.Parent = frame
    corner(icon, 5)
    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -36, 1, 0)
    label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 0)
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.Text = "LZ7 BLOX | 60 FPS"
    label.TextColor3 = Theme.text
    label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    label.TextSize = 11
    label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    label.Parent = frame
    local lastTime = tick()
    local frames = 0
    RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        frames = frames + 1
        if tick() - lastTime >= 1 then
            label.Text = "LZ7 BLOX | " .. frames .. " FPS"
            frames = 0
            lastTime = tick()
        end
    end)
end

        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            dragging = true

                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then dragging = false end
            end)
        end
    end)

        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then dragInput = input end

        if input == dragInput and dragging then
            local delta = input.Position - dragStart

            local maxH = math.max(leftLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y, rightLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
            page.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, maxH + 20)
        end
        leftLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)
        rightLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)

        return page, left, right
    end

    local function createNavBtn(tab, idx)
        local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        btn.Name = tab.name

        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard
        btn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        btn.AutoButtonColor = false
        btn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        btn.Text = ""
        btn.Parent = navScroll
        corner(btn, 8)

        local activeBar = Instance.new("Frame")
        activeBar.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 20)
        activeBar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -10)
        activeBar.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent
        activeBar.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        activeBar.BorderSizePixel = 0
        activeBar.Parent = btn
        corner(activeBar, 2)

        local iconBox = Instance.new("Frame")
        iconBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 26)
        iconBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -13)
        iconBox.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard
        iconBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
        iconBox.Parent = btn
        corner(iconBox, 6)
        stroke(iconBox, Theme.border, 1, 0.5)

        local iconLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        iconLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        iconLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        iconLbl.Text = tab.letter
        iconLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted
        iconLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        iconLbl.TextSize = 12
        iconLbl.Parent = iconBox

        local nameLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        nameLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -46, 1, 0)
        nameLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 0)
        nameLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        nameLbl.Text = tab.name
        nameLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted
        nameLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        nameLbl.TextSize = 12
        nameLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        nameLbl.Parent = btn

        local function setActive(active)
            if active then
                tween(btn, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCardActive, BackgroundTransparency = 0}, 0.25)
                tween(iconBox, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent}, 0.25)
                tween(iconLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textBright}, 0.25)
                tween(nameLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.text}, 0.25)
                tween(activeBar, {BackgroundTransparency = 0}, 0.25)
                local s = iconBox:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
                if s then tween(s, {Color = Theme.accentBright, Transparency = 0.2}, 0.25) end
            else
                tween(btn, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.25)
                tween(iconBox, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard}, 0.25)
                tween(iconLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.25)
                tween(nameLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.25)
                tween(activeBar, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.25)
                local s = iconBox:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
                if s then tween(s, {Color = Theme.border, Transparency = 0.5}, 0.25) end
            end
        end

        btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if activeNav ~= btn then
                tween(btn, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCardHover, BackgroundTransparency = 0.3}, 0.15)
                tween(nameLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textSub}, 0.15)
                tween(iconLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textSub}, 0.15)
            end
        end)
        btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if activeNav ~= btn then
                tween(btn, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.15)
                tween(nameLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.15)
                tween(iconLbl, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.15)
            end
        end)

        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            for _, c in pairs(navScroll:GetChildren()) do
                if c:IsA("TextButton") and c ~= btn then
                    tween(c, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.2)
                    for _, d in pairs(c:GetDescendants()) do
                        if d:IsA("TextLabel") then tween(d, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.2)
                        elseif d:IsA("Frame") and d.Size.X.Offset == 26 then tween(d, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard}, 0.2)
                        elseif d:IsA("Frame") and d.Size.X.Offset == 3 then tween(d, {BackgroundTransparency = 1}, 0.2)
                        elseif d:IsA("UIStroke") then tween(d, {Color = Theme.border, Transparency = 0.5}, 0.2) end
                    end
                end
            end
            for _, p in pairs(tabPages) do
                if p.page ~= tabPages[tab.name].page then p.page.Visible = false end
            end
            if tabPages[tab.name] then
                local newPage = tabPages[tab.name].page
                newPage.Visible = true
                newPage.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 0)
                tween(newPage, {Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)}, 0.3)
            end
            sectionTitle.Text = tab.name:upper()
            sectionDesc.Text = tab.desc
            setActive(true)
            activeNav = btn
        end)

        return btn, setActive
    end

    local function createSection(parent, title)
        local section = Instance.new("Frame")
        section.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0)
        section.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard
        section.BorderSizePixel = 0
        section.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        section.Parent = parent
        corner(section, 10)
        stroke(section, Theme.border, 1, 0.5)

        local hdr = Instance.new("Frame")
        hdr.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 36)
        hdr.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        hdr.Parent = section

        local acc = Instance.new("Frame")
        acc.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 14)
        acc.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -7)
        acc.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent
        acc.BorderSizePixel = 0
        acc.Parent = hdr
        corner(acc, 2)

        local titleLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        titleLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -30, 1, 0)
        titleLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 0)
        titleLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        titleLbl.Text = title
        titleLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.text
        titleLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        titleLbl.TextSize = 12
        titleLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        titleLbl.Parent = hdr

        local content = Instance.new("Frame")
        content.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 0)
        content.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 36)
        content.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        content.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
        content.Parent = section

        local cLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
        cLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 6)
        cLayout.Parent = content

        local cPad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        cPad.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 10)
        cPad.Parent = content

        return content
    end

    local function createToggle(parent, title, default, callback)
        local row = Instance.new("TextButton")
        row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34)
        row.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput
        row.AutoButtonColor = false
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.Text = ""
        row.Parent = parent
        corner(row, 6)
        stroke(row, Theme.border, 1, 0.6)

        local titleLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        titleLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -54, 1, 0)
        titleLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        titleLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        titleLbl.Text = title
        titleLbl.TextColor3 = default and Theme.text or Theme.textSub
        titleLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        titleLbl.TextSize = 11
        titleLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        titleLbl.Parent = row

        local pill = Instance.new("Frame")
        pill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 16)
        pill.Position = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0.5, -8)
        pill.BackgroundColor3 = default and Theme.accent or Theme.bgCard
        pill.BorderSizePixel = 0
        pill.Parent = row
        corner(pill, 8)

        local knob = Instance.new("Frame")
        knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
        knob.Position = default and UDim2.new(1, -14, 0.5, -6) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -6)
        knob.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.textBright
        knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        knob.Parent = pill
        corner(knob, 6)

        local state = default

        row.MouseEnter:Connect(function() tween(row, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCardHover}, 0.15) end)
        row.MouseLeave:Connect(function() tween(row, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput}, 0.15) end)

        row.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            state = not state
            tween(pill, {BackgroundColor3 = state and Theme.accent or Theme.bgCard}, 0.25)
            tween(knob, {Position = state and UDim2.new(1, -14, 0.5, -6) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -6)}, 0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Back)
            tween(titleLbl, {TextColor3 = state and Theme.text or Theme.textSub}, 0.2)
            callback(state)
        end)

        return row
    end

    local function createSlider(parent, title, min, max, default, unit, callback)
        local card = Instance.new("Frame")
        card.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 56)
        card.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput
        card.BorderSizePixel = 0
        card.Parent = parent
        corner(card, 6)
        stroke(card, Theme.border, 1, 0.6)

        local titleLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        titleLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 0, 16)
        titleLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 8)
        titleLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        titleLbl.Text = title
        titleLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textSub
        titleLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        titleLbl.TextSize = 11
        titleLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        titleLbl.Parent = card

        local valueLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        valueLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 16)
        valueLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -78, 0, 8)
        valueLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        valueLbl.Text = tostring(default) .. (unit or "")
        valueLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.accentBright
        valueLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        valueLbl.TextSize = 11
        valueLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        valueLbl.Parent = card

        local sliderBg = Instance.new("Frame")
        sliderBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 4)
        sliderBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 36)
        sliderBg.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCard
        sliderBg.BorderSizePixel = 0
        sliderBg.Parent = card
        corner(sliderBg, 2)

        local pct = (default - min) / (max - min)

        local fill = Instance.new("Frame")
        fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
        fill.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent
        fill.BorderSizePixel = 0
        fill.Parent = sliderBg
        corner(fill, 2)
        gradient(fill, {
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Theme.accent),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Theme.accentBright)
        }, 0)

        local knob = Instance.new("TextButton")
        knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14)
        knob.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -7, 0.5, -7)
        knob.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.textBright
        knob.Text = ""
        knob.AutoButtonColor = false
        knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
        knob.ZIndex = 10
        knob.Parent = sliderBg
        corner(knob, 7)
        stroke(knob, Theme.accent, 2, 0.2)

        local dragging = false
        local current = default

        local function update(input)
            local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
            local sliderPos = sliderBg.AbsolutePosition
            local sliderSize = sliderBg.AbsoluteSize.X
            local relX = math.clamp(mousePos.X - sliderPos.X, 0, sliderSize)
            local percent = relX / sliderSize
            local value = math.floor(min + (max - min) * percent + 0.5)
            value = math.clamp(value, min, max)
            if value ~= current then
                current = value
                local newPct = (value - min) / (max - min)
                tween(fill, {Size = UDim2.new(newPct, 0, 1, 0)}, 0.1)
                tween(knob, {Position = UDim2.new(newPct, -7, 0.5, -7)}, 0.1)
                valueLbl.Text = tostring(value) .. (unit or "")
                callback(value)
            end
        end

        knob.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
            dragging = true
            tween(knob, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18), Position = UDim2.new((current-min)/(max-min), -9, 0.5, -9)}, 0.15)
        end)

        sliderBg.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                dragging = true
                update(input)
            end
        end)

        UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                if dragging then
                    tween(knob, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14), Position = UDim2.new((current-min)/(max-min), -7, 0.5, -7)}, 0.15)
                end
                dragging = false
            end
        end)

        UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
            if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then update(input) end
        end)

        return card
    end

    local function createDropdown(parent, title, options, default, callback)
        local row = Instance.new("TextButton")
        row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34)
        row.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput
        row.AutoButtonColor = false
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.Text = ""
        row.Parent = parent
        corner(row, 6)
        stroke(row, Theme.border, 1, 0.6)

        local titleLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        titleLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1, 0)
        titleLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
        titleLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        titleLbl.Text = title
        titleLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textSub
        titleLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        titleLbl.TextSize = 11
        titleLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        titleLbl.Parent = row

        local valueLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        valueLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -28, 1, 0)
        valueLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, 0)
        valueLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        valueLbl.Text = options[default or 1]
        valueLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.accentBright
        valueLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        valueLbl.TextSize = 11
        valueLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        valueLbl.Parent = row

        local arrow = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        arrow.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 1, 0)
        arrow.Position = UDim2.new(1, -22, 0, 0)
        arrow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        arrow.Text = "v"
        arrow.TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted
        arrow.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        arrow.TextSize = 10
        arrow.Parent = row

        local idx = default or 1

        row.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            tween(row, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgCardHover}, 0.15)
            tween(arrow, {TextColor3 = Theme.accent}, 0.15)
        end)
        row.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            tween(row, {BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput}, 0.15)
            tween(arrow, {TextColor3 = Theme.textMuted}, 0.15)
        end)

        row.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            idx = idx + 1
            if idx > #options then idx = 1 end
            valueLbl.Text = options[idx]
            tween(arrow, {Rotation = arrow.Rotation + 180}, 0.3)
            callback(options[idx])
        end)

        return row
    end

    -- CRIAR PÁGINAS
    for i, tab in ipairs(tabs) do
        local page, left, right = createPage(tab.name)
        tabPages[tab.name] = {page = page, left = left, right = right}
        createNavBtn(tab, i)
    end

    -- COMBAT
    local combatL = tabPages["Combat"].left
    local combatR = tabPages["Combat"].right

    local aimSec = createSection(combatL, "AIMBOT")
    createToggle(aimSec, "Enable Aimbot", false, function(v) CONFIG.aimEnabled = v end)
    createToggle(aimSec, "Wall Check", true, function(v) CONFIG.aimWallCheck = v end)
    createToggle(aimSec, "Team Check", true, function(v) CONFIG.teamCheck = v end)
    createDropdown(aimSec, "Aim Key", {"F", "V", "Right Click", "Always"}, 1, function(v)
        if v == "F" then CONFIG.aimKey = "F"
        elseif v == "V" then CONFIG.aimKey = "V"
        elseif v == "Right Click" then CONFIG.aimKey = "MouseButton2"
        elseif v == "Always" then CONFIG.aimKey = "always" end
    end)

    local fovSec = createSection(combatL, "FOV & PRECISION")
    createSlider(fovSec, "FOV Radius", 50, 500, 150, "px", function(v) CONFIG.aimFOV = v end)
    createSlider(fovSec, "Smoothness", 1, 30, 15, "%", function(v) CONFIG.smoothness = v end)
    createToggle(fovSec, "Show FOV Circle", false, function(v) CONFIG.showFOV = v end)

    local silentSec = createSection(combatR, "SILENT AIM")
    createToggle(silentSec, "Enable Silent Aim", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.silentAimEnabled = v
        if v then
            setupSilentAim()
            StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = "Silent Aim",
                Text = "Activated! Click to hit enemies.",
                Duration = 2,
                Icon = LZ7_ICON
            })
        else
            if silentAimConnection then silentAimConnection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end)
    createToggle(silentSec, "Requires Aimbot ON", false, function(v) CONFIG.aimEnabled = v end)

    -- VISUALS
    local visL = tabPages["Visuals"].left
    local visR = tabPages["Visuals"].right

    local espSec = createSection(visL, "ESP MAIN")
    createToggle(espSec, "Enable ESP", false, function(v) CONFIG.espEnabled = v end)
    createToggle(espSec, "Team Check", true, function(v) CONFIG.teamCheck = v end)
    createSlider(espSec, "Max Distance", 100, 5000, 1000, "m", function(v) CONFIG.espDistance = v end)

    local espOpts = createSection(visR, "ESP OPTIONS")
    createToggle(espOpts, "Box ESP", true, function(v) CONFIG.espBox = v end)
    createToggle(espOpts, "Tracer Lines", true, function(v) CONFIG.espTracer = v end)
    createToggle(espOpts, "Name Tags", true, function(v) CONFIG.espName = v end)
    createToggle(espOpts, "Health Bars", true, function(v) CONFIG.espHealth = v end)

    -- MOVEMENT
    local movL = tabPages["Movement"].left
    local movR = tabPages["Movement"].right

    local speedSec = createSection(movL, "SPEED & JUMP")
    createToggle(speedSec, "Walk Speed Mod", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.speedEnabled = v
        if localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = v and CONFIG.walkSpeed or 16
        end
    end)
    createSlider(speedSec, "Walk Speed", 16, 200, 16, "", function(v)
        CONFIG.walkSpeed = v
        if CONFIG.speedEnabled and localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = v
        end
    end)
    createToggle(speedSec, "Jump Power Mod", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.jumpEnabled = v
        if localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = v and CONFIG.jumpPower or 50
        end
    end)
    createSlider(speedSec, "Jump Power", 50, 500, 50, "", function(v)
        CONFIG.jumpPower = v
        if CONFIG.jumpEnabled and localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = v
        end
    end)

    local clipSec = createSection(movR, "CLIPPING")
    createToggle(clipSec, "Noclip", false, function(v) CONFIG.noclip = v end)
    createToggle(clipSec, "Infinite Jump", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.infiniteJump = v
        infiniteJumpActive = v
    end)

    -- CAMERA
    local camL = tabPages["Camera"].left
    local camR = tabPages["Camera"].right

    local viewSec = createSection(camL, "CAMERA VIEW")
    createToggle(viewSec, "Third Person", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.thirdPerson = v
        if v then
            thirdPersonActive = true
            originalCameraSubject = Camera.CameraSubject
            Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable
        else
            thirdPersonActive = false
            Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
            Camera.CameraSubject = originalCameraSubject
        end
    end)
    createSlider(viewSec, "Camera Distance", 4, 30, 8, "m", function(v) CONFIG.thirdPersonDistance = v end)

    local cursorSec = createSection(camR, "CURSOR")
    createToggle(cursorSec, "Free Cursor", false, function(v)
        if v ~= cursorUnlocked then toggleCursor() end
    end)

    -- EXPLOITS
    local expL = tabPages["Exploits"].left
    local expR = tabPages["Exploits"].right

    local btSec = createSection(expL, "BACKTRACK")
    createToggle(btSec, "Enable Backtrack", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.backtrackEnabled = v
        if not v then
            for _, indicators in pairs(backtrackIndicators) do
                for _, ind in pairs(indicators) do ind:Remove() end
            end
            backtrackIndicators = {}
            backtrackHistory = {}
        end
    end)
    createSlider(btSec, "Ticks", 1, 20, 8, "", function(v) CONFIG.backtrackTicks = v end)
    createSlider(btSec, "Time Window", 5, 50, 20, "0ms", function(v) CONFIG.backtrackTime = v / 100 end)
    createToggle(btSec, "Show Indicators", true, function(v) CONFIG.backtrackIndicator = v end)

    local lagSec = createSection(expR, "FAKE LAG")
    createToggle(lagSec, "Enable Fake Lag", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.fakeLagEnabled = v
        if v then startFakeLag() else stopFakeLag() end
    end)
    createDropdown(lagSec, "Mode", {"Teleport", "Rubberband", "Stutter"}, 1, function(v)
        CONFIG.fakeLagMode = v
        if CONFIG.fakeLagEnabled then stopFakeLag(); startFakeLag() end
    end)
    createSlider(lagSec, "Delay", 10, 150, 30, "0ms", function(v)
        CONFIG.fakeLagDelay = v / 100
        if CONFIG.fakeLagEnabled then stopFakeLag(); startFakeLag() end
    end)
    createSlider(lagSec, "Intensity", 1, 15, 5, "", function(v) CONFIG.fakeLagIntensity = v end)

    -- SETTINGS
    local setL = tabPages["Settings"].left
    local setR = tabPages["Settings"].right

    local perfSec = createSection(setL, "PERFORMANCE")
    createToggle(perfSec, "FPS Boost", false, function(v)
        CONFIG.optimizeFPS = v
        if v then
            Lighting.GlobalShadows = false
            Lighting.Brightness = 2
        else
            Lighting.GlobalShadows = true
        end
    end)
    createToggle(perfSec, "Show Watermark", true, function(v)
        CONFIG.showWatermark = v
        if watermarkGui then watermarkGui.Enabled = v end
    end)

    local kbSec = createSection(setR, "KEYBINDS")

    local function addKb(parent, key, action)
        local row = Instance.new("Frame")
        row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 28)
        row.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.bgInput
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.Parent = parent
        corner(row, 6)

        local kBox = Instance.new("Frame")
        kBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 20)
        kBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, -10)
        kBox.BackgroundColor3 = Theme.accent
        kBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
        kBox.Parent = row
        corner(kBox, 4)

        local kLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        kLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        kLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        kLbl.Text = key
        kLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textBright
        kLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        kLbl.TextSize = 10
        kLbl.Parent = kBox

        local actLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        actLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -50, 1, 0)
        actLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 48, 0, 0)
        actLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        actLbl.Text = action
        actLbl.TextColor3 = Theme.textSub
        actLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        actLbl.TextSize = 10
        actLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        actLbl.Parent = row
    end

    addKb(kbSec, "U", "Toggle Menu")
    addKb(kbSec, "P", "Free Cursor")
    addKb(kbSec, "F", "Aim Head")
    addKb(kbSec, "V", "Aim Body")

    -- WINDOW BUTTONS
    makeWinBtn(Theme.close, function()
        tween(main, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0), Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)}, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In)
        task.wait(0.3)
        main.Visible = false
        menuVisible = false
        main.Size = UDim2.new(0, 680, 0, 460)
        main.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -340, 0.5, -230)
        UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = cursorUnlocked
    end)

    makeWinBtn(Theme.minimize, function()
        minimized = not minimized
        if minimized then
            tween(main, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 110)}, 0.3)
            contentArea.Visible = false
            navScroll.Visible = false
            sep1.Visible = false
        else
            tween(main, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 680, 0, 460)}, 0.3)
            task.wait(0.2)
            contentArea.Visible = true
            navScroll.Visible = true
            sep1.Visible = true
        end
    end)

    makeWinBtn(Theme.maximize, function() end)

    task.defer(function()
        local firstBtn = navScroll:FindFirstChild("Combat")
        if firstBtn then firstBtn.MouseButton1Click:Fire() end
    end)

    local function openMenu()
        main.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        main.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
        main.Visible = true
        tween(main, {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 680, 0, 460),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -340, 0.5, -230)
        }, 0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Back)
    end

    return main, openMenu
end

    if not gp and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.U then
        if mainFrame then
            menuVisible = not menuVisible
            if menuVisible then
                openMenuFn()
                UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = true
            else
                tween(mainFrame, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0), Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)}, 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In)
                task.wait(0.3)
                mainFrame.Visible = false
                mainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 680, 0, 460)
                mainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -340, 0.5, -230)
                UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = cursorUnlocked
            end
        end
    end
end)

end)

        local hrp = localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
        local offset = Vector3.new(0, 2, CONFIG.thirdPersonDistance)
        Camera.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position + offset, hrp.Position)
    end
end)

    if CONFIG.noclip and localPlayer.Character then
        for _, part in ipairs(localPlayer.Character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then part.CanCollide = false end
        end
    end
end)

    if infiniteJumpActive and localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
        localPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
    end
end)

    if espTable[player] then
        for _, d in pairs(espTable[player]) do pcall(function() d:Remove() end) end
        espTable[player] = nil
    end
end)

local oldNamecall
oldNamecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self, ...)
    local method = getnamecallmethod()
    if method == "Kick" and self == localPlayer then
        return nil
    end
    return oldNamecall(self, ...)
end))

local oldFireServer
oldFireServer = hookfunction(Instance.new("RemoteEvent").FireServer, newcclosure(function(self, ...)
    if typeof(self) == "Instance" then
        local s, name = pcall(function() return self.Name end)
        if s then
            if name == "Ban" or name == "Kick" or name == "ServerBan" or name == "Ping" or name == "Flashlight" or name == "ShockPlayer" or name == "RemoteEv3e1nt" or name == "FallDam3a1ge" or name == "BURN1M4E" then
                return nil
            end
        end
    end
    return oldFireServer(self, ...)
end))

-- Fix: override refreshConfigs to handle both / and \ path separators
function library:refreshConfigs()
    local tbl = {}
    for i,v in next, listfiles("alora/"..tostring(game.GameId)) do
        local parts = v:split("/")
        local filename = parts[#parts]
        -- also handle backslash
        local bparts = filename:split("\\")
        filename = bparts[#bparts]
        -- remove .cfg extension
        local name = filename:split(".")[1]
        if name and name ~= "" then
            table.insert(tbl, name)
        end
    end
    library.options["selected_config"].refresh(tbl)
end

    label.Text = name
    label.TextSize = 13
    label.Visible = true
    label.Parent = specList
end

function removeSpectators()
    for _, child in next, specList:GetChildren() do
        if child:IsA("TextLabel") then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end
end

--functions
function encodePos(pos)
    return Vector3.new(((pos.X - 74312) * 4 + 1325) * 13,(pos.Y + 3183421) * 4 - 4201432,(pos.Z * 41 - 581357) * 2)
end

function decodePos(encodedPos)
    return Vector3.new(((encodedPos.X / 13 - 1325) / 4) + 74312,((encodedPos.Y + 4201432) / 4) - 3183421,((encodedPos.Z / 2 + 581357) / 41))
end

function isAlive(plr)
    if not plr then plr = localPlayer end
    return plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and plr.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and true or false
end

function hasProperty(ins,pro)
    return pcall(function() _=ins[pro] end)
end

function getWeaponInfo()
    local information = {
        alive = isAlive()
    }
    if not information.alive then return information end
    if replicatedStorage.Weapons:FindFirstChild(localPlayer.Character.EquippedTool.Value) then
        local weapType = "other"
        local hitboxes = {}
        local weapon = replicatedStorage.Weapons[localPlayer.Character.EquippedTool.Value]
        if weapon:FindFirstChild("RifleThing") then
            weapType = "rifle"
        elseif weapon:FindFirstChild("Secondary") and weapon.Name ~= "R8" and weapon.Name ~= "DesertEagle" then
            weapType = "pistol"
        elseif weapon.Name == "R8" or weapon.Name == "DesertEagle" then
            weapType = "heavyp"
        elseif weapon.Name == "AWP" then
            weapType = "awp"
        elseif weapon.Name == "Scout" then
            weapType = "scout"
        end

        for i,v in next, library.flags[weapType.."_hitboxes"] do
            for _i,_v in next, hitboxList[v] do
                table.insert(hitboxes,_v)
            end
        end

        information["name"] = weapon.Name
        information["melee"] = false
        information["aim_assist"] = library.flags[weapType.."_assist"]
        information["silent_aim"] = library.flags[weapType.."_silent"]
        information["triggerbot"] = library.flags[weapType.."_triggerbot"]
        information["assist_fov"] = library.flags[weapType.."_assist_fov"]
        information["silent_fov"] = library.flags[weapType.."_silent_fov"]
        information["smoothness"] = library.flags[weapType.."_assist_smoothness"]
        information["trigger_delay"] = library.flags[weapType.."_triggerdelay"]
        information["hitboxes"] = hitboxes
    end
    return information
end

function teamCheck(plr,team)
    return plr ~= localPlayer and team or plr.Team ~= localPlayer.Team
end

function getNearest(visOnly,team)
    local player,nearest = nil,9e9
    for i,v in next, players:GetPlayers() do
        if teamCheck(v,team) and isAlive(v) then
            if visOnly then
                local ray = Ray.new(camera.CFrame.p,(v.Character.Head.Position - camera.CFrame.p).unit * 500)
                local hit,_ = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(ray, {camera,localPlayer.Character,workspace.Ray_Ignore,workspace.Map.Clips,workspace.Map.SpawnPoints})
                if hit and hit:IsDescendantOf(v.Character) then else continue end
            end
            local screenPos,onScreen = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
            local magnitude = (Vector2.new(screenPos.X,screenPos.Y)-Vector2.new(mouse.X,mouse.Y)).magnitude
            if onScreen and magnitude < nearest then
                player = v
                nearest = magnitude
            end
        end
    end
    return player,nearest
end

function isButtonDown(key)
    if string.find(tostring(key),"KeyCode") then
        return userInputService:IsKeyDown(key) 
    else
        for _,v in pairs(userInputService:GetMouseButtonsPressed()) do
            if v.UserInputType == key then
                return true
            end
        end
    end
	return false
end

function updateSkybox()
    if lighting:FindFirstChild("customsky") then
        lighting.customsky:Destroy()
    end
    if lighting:FindFirstChild("SunRays") then
        lighting.SunRays.Enabled = false
    end
    local customsky = Instance.new("Sky",lighting)
    customsky.Name = "customsky"
    customsky.SunTextureId = "rbxassetid://"
    customsky.CelestialBodiesShown = "rbxassetid://"
    if library.flags["skybox_changer"] and skyboxes[library.flags["selected_skybox"]] then
        for i,v in next, skyboxes[library.flags["selected_skybox"]] do
            customsky[i] = v
        end
    end
end

local tracerDebounce = false
function createTracer(to,from)
    if not tracerDebounce then
        tracerDebounce = true
        spawn(function()
            wait()
            tracerDebounce = false
        end)
        to -= (from.Position - to).unit*100
        local part1 = Instance.new("Part")
        local part2 = Instance.new("Part")
        local beam = Instance.new("Beam",part1)
        local beam2 = Instance.new("Beam",part1)
        local attachment1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
        local attachment2 = Instance.new("Attachment")

        part1.Transparency = 1;part1.Position = to;part1.CanCollide = false;part1.Anchored = true;part1.Parent = workspace.Debris;attachment1.Parent = part1
        part2.Transparency = 1;part2.Position = from.Position;part2.CanCollide = false;part2.Anchored = true;part2.Parent = workspace.Debris;attachment2.Parent = part2
        beam.FaceCamera = true;beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(library.flags["tracer_color"]);beam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new{NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,1-0.5),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1-0.5)};beam.Width0 = 0.055;beam.Width1 = 0.055;beam.LightEmission = 1;beam.LightInfluence = 0;beam.Attachment0 = attachment1;beam.Attachment1 = attachment2;beam.Parent = part1
        beam2.FaceCamera = true;beam2.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1));beam2.Transparency = NumberSequence.new{NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,1-0.75),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1-0.75)};beam2.Width0 = 0.025;beam2.Width1 = 0.025;beam2.LightEmission = 1;beam2.LightInfluence = 0;beam2.Attachment0 = attachment1;beam2.Attachment1 = attachment2;beam2.Parent = part1
        
        spawn(function()
            wait(2)
            for i=0.5,0,-0.025 do wait()
                beam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new{NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,1-i),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1-i)}
                beam2.Transparency = NumberSequence.new{NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,(0.75)-i),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,(0.75)-i)}
            end
            for i=0.25,0,-0.025 do wait()
                beam2.Transparency = NumberSequence.new{NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,1-i),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1-i)}
            end
            beam:Destroy()
            beam2:Destroy()
        end)
    end
end

local espObjects = {}
function createEsp(plr)
    if plr == localPlayer then return end
    local textDropShadowESP = Drawing.new("Text")
    local textESP = Drawing.new("Text")
    local boxESP = Drawing.new("Square")
    local boxoutlineESP = Drawing.new("Square")
    local boxinlineESP = Drawing.new("Square")
    local healthbarESPoutline = Drawing.new("Square")
    local healthbarESP = Drawing.new("Square")

    textESP.Font = Drawing.Fonts.Plex
    textESP.Size = 16
    textESP.Color = Color3.new(1,1,1)
    textESP.OutlineColor = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    textESP.Transparency = 1

    textDropShadowESP.Font = Drawing.Fonts.Plex
    textDropShadowESP.Size = 16
    textDropShadowESP.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    textDropShadowESP.OutlineColor = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    textDropShadowESP.Transparency = 1

    boxESP.Thickness = 1
    boxESP.Color = Color3.new(1,1,1)
    boxESP.Transparency = 1

    boxoutlineESP.Thickness = 1
    boxoutlineESP.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    boxoutlineESP.Transparency = 1

    boxinlineESP.Thickness = 1
    boxinlineESP.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    boxinlineESP.Transparency = 1
    
    healthbarESP.Thickness = 1
    healthbarESP.Color = Color3.fromRGB(50,220,50)
    healthbarESP.Transparency = 1

    healthbarESPoutline.Thickness = 1
    healthbarESPoutline.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    healthbarESPoutline.Transparency = 1
    healthbarESPoutline.Filled = true

    function invis()
        textESP.Visible = false
        textDropShadowESP.Visible = false
        boxESP.Visible = false
        boxoutlineESP.Visible = false
        boxinlineESP.Visible = false
        healthbarESPoutline.Visible = false
        healthbarESP.Visible = false
    end

    function remove()
        textESP:Remove()
        textDropShadowESP:Remove()
        boxESP:Remove()
        boxoutlineESP:Remove()
        healthbarESP:Remove()
        boxinlineESP:Remove()
        healthbarESPoutline:Remove()
        healthbarESP:Remove()
        espObjects[plr.Name] = nil
    end

    local espList = {
        text = textESP,
        textshadow = textDropShadowESP,
        box = boxESP,
        boxol = boxoutlineESP,
        boxil = boxinlineESP,
        healthb = healthbarESP,
        healthbo = healthbarESPoutline,

        invis = invis,
        remove = remove,
    }
    espObjects[plr.Name] = espList
end

function getOffsets(x,y,minY,z)
    return {CFrame.new(x,y,z),CFrame.new(-x,y,z),CFrame.new(x,y,-z),CFrame.new(-x,y,-z),CFrame.new(x,-minY,z),CFrame.new(-x,-minY,z),CFrame.new(x,-minY,-z),CFrame.new(-x,-minY,-z)}
end

function floor(val)
    return Vector2.new(math.floor(val.X),math.floor(val.Y))
end

function updateViewmodel()
    if camera:FindFirstChild("Arms") then
        local arms = camera.Arms
        for i,v in next, arms:GetChildren() do
            if library.flags["weapon_chams"] then
                if (v:IsA("MeshPart") or v.Name == "Part") and v.Transparency ~= 1 then
                    if v.Name == "StatClock" then v:ClearAllChildren() end
                    v.Color = library.flags["weapon_color"]
                    v.Transparency = library.flags["weapon_trans"]/100
                    v.Material = "SmoothPlastic"
                    if hasProperty(v,"TextureID") then v.TextureID = "" end
                end
            end
            if v:IsA"Model" then
                for _i,_v in next, v:GetDescendants() do
                    if library.flags["remove_sleeves"] and _v.Name == "Sleeve" then
                        _v:Destroy()
                    end
                    if library.flags["arm_chams"] then
                        if hasProperty(_v,"CastShadow") then _v.CastShadow = false end
                        if _v:IsA"SpecialMesh" then
                            local clr = library.flags["arm_color"]
                            _v.VertexColor = Vector3.new(clr.R,clr.G,clr.B)
                        end
                        if _v:IsA"Part" then
                            _v.Material = "SmoothPlastic"
                            _v.Transparency = library.flags["arm_trans"]/100
                            _v.Color = library.flags["arm_color"]
                            if _v.Transparency == 1 then continue end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

local btInfo = {parent = nil,folder = nil}

local silentPart = nil
local hookJp = nil
local hookWs = nil
local timeout = 0

local oldNewindex
oldNewindex = hookmetamethod(game, "__newindex", newcclosure(function(self,idx,val)
    if not checkcaller() then return oldNewindex(self,idx,val) end
    if idx == "JumpPower" and hookJp then
        val = 22
    end
    return oldNewindex(self,idx,val)
end))

--[[local namecallOld
namecallOld = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", newcclosure(function(self,...)
    local argsCount = select("#", ...)
    local args = {...}
    local method = getnamecallmethod()

    if not checkcaller() then return namecallOld(self, ...) end

    if method == "Kick" then 
        return 
    end
    if self.Name == "RemoteEvent" and typeof(args[1]) == "table" and args[1][1] == "kick" then
        return
    end
    if self.Name == "FallDamage" and library.flags["fall_damage"] then
        return
    end
    if self.Name == "BURNME" and library.flags["fire_damage"] then
        return
    end
    if method == "InvokeServer" and self.Name == "Hugh" then
        return
    end

    if string.find(method,"IgnoreList") and silentPart then
        args[1] = Ray.new(camera.CFrame.p, (silentPart.Position + Vector3.new(0,(camera.CFrame.p-silentPart.Position).Magnitude/500,0) - camera.CFrame.p).unit * 500)
    end

    if typeof(self) == "Instance" and (method == "SetPrimaryPartCFrame" or method == "PivotTo") and library.flags["viewmodel_changer"] then
        local viewmodelCFrame = args[1]
        if typeof(viewmodelCFrame) == "CFrame" then
            viewmodelCFrame *= CFrame.new((library.flags["viewmodel_x"]-20)/10,(library.flags["viewmodel_y"]-20)/10,(library.flags["viewmodel_z"]-20)/10)
            args[1] = viewmodelCFrame
        end
    end

    if method == "FireServer" then
        if args[1] == localPlayer.UserId or string.find(tostring(args[1]),'{') then
            return
        end
        if not btInfo.parent and self.Name == "RemoteEvent" and typeof(args[1]) == "table" and tostring(args[1][3]) == "btp" then
            btInfo.parent = args[1][3].read.Value
            btInfo.folder = args[1][3].Parent
            spawn(function()
                wait()
                btInfo.parent = nil
            end)
            return
        end
        if self.Name == "ApplyGun" then
            if string.find(args[1],"Banana") or string.find(args[1],"Flip") then 
                args[1] = localPlayer.Status.Team.Value.." Knife"
            end
        end
        if self.Name == "HitParl" then
            if timeout > 0 then
                return
            end
            if string.find(string.lower(args[1].Name),"head") then
                timeout = 7
            end
            spawn(function()
                local hitplayer = players:FindFirstChild(args[1].Parent.Name)
                if hitplayer then
                    preventBt = true
                    wait()
                    preventBt = false
                end
                if library.flags["hitsound_enabled"] and hitplayer and teamCheck(hitplayer,false) then
                    local hitsound = Instance.new("Sound",workspace)
                    hitsound.SoundId = hitsounds[library.flags["hitsound_value"]
                    hitsound.PlayOnRemove = true
                    hitsound.Volume = library.flags["hitsound_volume"]
                    hitsound:Destroy()
                end
                if library.flags["bullet_tracer"] and localPlayer.Character and  camera:FindFirstChild("Arms") then
                    local from = camera.Arms:FindFirstChild("Flash")
                    if from then
                        createTracer(decodePos(args[2]),from)
                    end
                end
            end
            if btInfo.parent and not preventBt then
                args[1] = btInfo.parent.Head
                args[2] = encodePos(args[1].Position)
                timeout = 7
                btInfo.parent = nil
                spawn(function()
                    btInfo.folder:ClearAllChildren()
                end)
            end
        end
    end
    return namecallOld(self, table.unpack(args, 1, argsCount))
end--]]
